1 2015 Sustainability Report Motif Batik Wakaroros Dayak Basap dari Kutai Timur Sungguh suatu kehormatan bagi KPC telah diberikan kepercayaan Wakaroros Batik Motif which is originated by Dayak Basap Tribe oleh Indonesia untuk mengelola of East Kutai kekayaan sumber daya batubara negeri ini. Oleh karena itu, tidak hanya menambang, apa yang kami kelola di Sangatta harus mampu memberikan manfaat yang berkelanjutan bagi seluruh pemangku kepentingan, berkontribusi dalam pembangunan manusia Indonesia, dan pembangunan nasional negeri ini. Semangat kami membara untuk Indonesia. It is our greatest honor and privilege to bear the trust of the government and the people of Indonesia to manage the country’s vast coal resources. Therefore, more than mining, our operation must be able to provide sustainable benefits to all stakeholders and contribute to Indonesia’s society and national development. Our burning spirit for Indonesia. Laporan ini adalah wujud komitmen dan tanggung jawab kami kepada seluruh pemangku kepentingan, sekaligus wujud Tentang Laporan Ini peran aktif KPC dalam upaya masyarakat global dalam mewujudkan masa depan yang lebih baik bagi generasi mendatang. — About This Report  This report represents our commitment and responsibility to all of our stakeholder, as well as as an embodiment of our active participation in global effort to create a better world for future generation. K PC telah secara konsisten menerbitkan Laporan Keberlanjutan secara tahunan K PC has been publishing our Annual Sustainability Report since 2003. This year is our 13th sejak 2003. Laporan ini adalah Sustainability Report, in which laporan kami yang ke-13 yang we have been transparently melanjutkan laporan keberlanjutan reporting information related to our tahun sebelumnya yang diterbitkan corporate sustainability strategy pada bulan Agustus 2015. Laporan dan performances. This report ini merangkum seluruh informasi is a continuity from our previous terkait strategi dan kinerja sustainability report that was keberlanjutan perusahaan. published in August 2015. Sustainable Partnership Siapa Pemangku Kepentingan Kami Who Are Our Stakeholders KPC mendefinisikan pemangku kepentingan sebagai individu KPC defines stakeholders as individuals or groups that Perubahan Signifikan & Pernyataan Ulang Significant Changes & Restatements atau kelompok yang dapat mempengaruhi atau dipengaruhi can affect or be affected by the our business. Principles KPC mengadopsi standar akuntansi baru, yakni PSAK24 KPC recently adopted a new accounting standard of kegiatan usaha Perusahaan. Prinsip pelibatan pemangku of stakeholders engagement implemented in KPC follow khususnya terkait kewajiban perusahaan atas post benefit PSAK24 regarding the company’s obligation towards kepentingan di KPC mengunakan prinsip sesuai dengan panduan the principles that are specified in Global Reporting karyawan. We operate one of the largest open-pit mining in the world. [G4-DMA][G4-56]  More Than Mining as our philosophy has led us to develop KPC a corporate initiative, called “SEMANGAT MEMBARA” (burning spirit) as the fundamental approach to achieve a more sustainable coal mining operation, which includes our entire coal chain, from the management, operation, customer, environment, safety and health, human resources, community, and supply chain. 36 Laporan Keberlanjutan 2015 37 2015 Sustainability Report SEMANGAT MEMBARA MEMBARA SPIRIT S ejak mulai penambangan pada tahun 1990, awal kegiatan operasional KPC selalu dilaksanakan dengan S ince 1990, which is the beginning of our operation, KPC always concerns on every aspects in the coal memperhatikan segala aspek yang chain. Hal ini sesuai dengan apa yang tertuang dalam Rencana Penutupan Tambang (RPT) KPC.  Sustainable development through community development programs is a commitment that we hold dear, monitor, and evaluate each year. In the implementation of community development programs, KPC acts as the catalyst for regional development. KPC collaborates with the government and communities to achieve results that benefit society with maximum efforts and well-aimed objectives, as well as encouraging the community independence by developing the existing potential. This is consistent with what is contained in the Mine Closure Plan (RPT) of KPC.socially and environmentally in the future. Forum MSH Penguatan Ekonomi Keluarga & Lokal Peningkatan Kualitas Hidup Masyarakat Masyarakat yang CSR Kutim (Tambang dan Non-Tambang) Berkelanjutan Penggunaan Lain (APL). Oleh public related to the operations of KPC are handled karena itu, KPC memiliki sistem pengelolaan bernama Community properly. Therefore, KPC has a management system Feedback System (Umpan Balik Masyarakat). CFS selalu memastikan called Community Feedback System. CFS always ensure semua keluhan dan teguran yang berasal dari masyarakat terkelola that all complaints and critics from the community are dengan baik dan diselesaikan sesuai dengan prosedur. managed and resolved according to the procedure. Menindaklanjuti data CFS tahun 2015, menunjukkan bahwa To follow-up CFS data in 2015, it is shown that blasting blasting dan konflik sosial menjadi keluhan utama yang terjadi and social conflict become major complaints that selama tahun 2015. Dari analisa lapangan dan data di atas, KPC occurred during 2015. Melakukan monitoring sosial dan lingkungan secara 01. Secara terus-menerus melakukan kegiatan kordinasi dan 02. Continually perform coordinating activities pertemuan dengan tokoh masyarakat dan pemerintah (desa, and meetings with community leaders and the kecamatan, kabupaten). government (village, sub-district, and district). 03. Kami selalu berusaha menjalin hubungan yang harmonis, adil, transparan dan bermanfaat keberlanjutan bagi kedua belah pihak untuk lebih memperkuat masing-masing bisnis yang dijalani dan memberikan keuntungan bagi para pemangku kepentingan. Pada tahun 2015, KPC didukung oleh 638 mitra pemasok jasa (kontraktor, baik penambangan maupun jasa lainnya) dan pemasok barang (supplier), baik dari lokal Kutai Timur, lokal Kalimantan Timur, nasional, dan luar negeri. [G4-EC9]  For us, the current development and advancement of KPC, are not separated from the efforts of partners who are jointly committed to achieve Good Mining Practice Implementation. We always try to establish a harmonious, fair, transparent relationship as well as beneficial to the sustainability of both parties to further strengthen their respective business and provide benefits for stakeholders.  In 2015, KPC was supported by 638 service suppliers (contractors, both mining and other services) and suppliers of goods, both from the local East Kutai, East Kalimantan, and national and foreign suppliers.
